JavaScript treats Array as Object only.\n\t\t// key\t\t\t: String\n\t\t// value\t\t: String\n\t\t// toArray\t\t: Boolean\n\t\t//\t\t\t\t  If true, creates an Array for duplicate entries\n\t\t//\t\t\t\t  If false, does not creat an Array for duplicate entries.
